***уложить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:уложить.html>уложи́ть</a> (3100)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">у-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">u-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">ложи́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ložítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:уложить.html>уложи́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">uložítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:укладывать.html>укла́дывать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to lay
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:уложить.html>уложи́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:постель.html>посте́ль</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">uložítʹ v postélʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to put to bed</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:уложить.html>уложи́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:место.html>ме́сте</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">uložítʹ na méste</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to kill on the spot</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to pack up</li>
<li>to stow, to pile, to stack</li>
<li><i>(hair)</i> to arrange, to style</li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:уложить.html>уложи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">uložítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:уложиться.html>уложи́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">uložítʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:укладываться.html>укла́дываться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to pack <i>(up)</i>, to be packing <i>(up)</i>, to be packing one's things</li>
<li>to go <i>(in, into)</i></li>
<li>to keep <i>(within)</i>, to confine oneself <i>(to)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:уложиться.html>уложи́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:графика.html>гра́фик</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>uložítʹsja</b> v gráfik</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">to be on schedule</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:уложиться.html>уложи́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:задать.html>за́данный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:срок.html>срок</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>uložítʹsja</b> v zádannyj srok</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">to meet the deadline</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мочь.html>мо́жет</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ли.html>ли</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:уложиться.html>уложи́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:десять.html>де́сять</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:минута.html>минут</a>?</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">móžet li on <b>uložítʹsja</b> v désjatʹ minut?</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">can he manage in ten minutes?; can he confine oneself to ten minutes?</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:уложить.html>уложи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">uložítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a><span class="hyph-dot" style="color:red;">·</span>ло<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:жить.html>жи́ть</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ся</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, непереходный,  <a href = vnd.unilang:возвратный.html>возвра́тный</a>,  <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 4c.      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:укладываться.html>укла́дываться</a>.

<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to like, to appreciate, to relish</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:улыбнуться.html>улыбну́ться</a> (619)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">улыбну́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ulybnútʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:улыбнуться.html>улыбну́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ulybnútʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:улыбаться.html>улыба́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to smile
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>она́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:украдкой.html>укра́дкой</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:улыбнуться.html>улыбну́лась</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:когда.html>когда́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:упасть.html>упа́л</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Oná ukrádkoj <b>ulybnúlasʹ</b>, kogdá on upál.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">She <b>smiled</b> furtively when he fell down.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl>
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2002</b>,  “<a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://lyricstranslate.com/ru/Zemfira-Paranoia-lyrics.html"><a href = vnd.unilang:паранойя.html>Парано́йя</a></a>”, performed by <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Zemfira" class="extiw" title="w:Zemfira">Zemfira</a>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:небо.html>не́бе</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:улыбнуться.html>улыбну́лись</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:звезда.html>звёзды</a></span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">A v nébe <b>ulybnúlisʹ</b> zvjózdy</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">And in the sky, the stars <b>smiled</b></span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">улыбну́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ulybnútʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a><span class="hyph-dot" style="color:red;">·</span>лыб<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ну́ть<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ся</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, непереходный,  <a href = vnd.unilang:возвратный.html>возвра́тный</a>,  <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 3b.      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:улыбаться.html>улыба́ться</a>.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-улыб-</b>; суффикс: <b>-ну</b>; глагольное <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ть</b>; постфикс: <b>-ся</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ум.html>ум</a> (630)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*umъ</i>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ум.html>ум</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">um</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ум.html>ума́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ум.html>умы́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ум.html>умо́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>mind
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:свое.html>своём</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ум.html>уме́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">v svojóm umé</i> ― <span class="e-translation">in one's senses, in one's right mind</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:свое.html>своём</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ум.html>уме́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ne v svojóm umé</i> ― <span class="e-translation">not right in the head, out of one's sense</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:взяться.html>взя́ться</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ум.html>ум</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">vzjátʹsja za <b>um</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">clean up one's act</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>него́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ум.html>ум</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:разум.html>ра́зум</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:зайти.html>зашёл</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">u nevó <b>um</b> za rázum zašól</i> ― <span class="e-translation">he got crazy</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прийти.html>прийти́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ум.html>ум</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">prijtí na <b>um</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to occur, to cross one's mind</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сводить.html>своди́ть</a>/<a href = vnd.unilang:свести.html>свести́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ум.html>ума́</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">svodítʹ/svestí s <b>umá</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to go crazy</span></div></dd></dl></li>

***умалять.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:умалять.html>умаля́ть</a> (31084)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">умали́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">umalítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-я́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-játʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:умалять.html>умаля́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">umaljátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">умали́ть</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to reduce, to lessen, to diminish</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively<span class="ib-comma">,</span> literary</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to reduce the role, the value or significance of</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">literary</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to belittle, to humiliate</li></ol>

***умение.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:умение.html>уме́ние</a> (3690)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:уметь.html>уме́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">umétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-е́ние</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-énije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:умение.html>уме́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">uménije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:умение.html>уме́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:умение.html>уме́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:умение.html>уме́ний</a></b>)
